# <a name="essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-103">Pagrindinės „Office“ paslaugos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-103">Essential services for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-104">Šiame straipsnyje pateikta informacija taikoma 1904 arba naujesnės versijos „Office“ kliento programinei įrangai, įdiegtai „Windows“ kompiuteryje:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-105">„Office 365 ProPlus“ ir „Office 365 Business“</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-106">„Office 365 Personal“, „Office 365 Home“ arba kitos „Office“ versijos, kurios yra „Office 365“ prenumeratos dalis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-107">„Project“ ir „Visio“, kurios įtrauktos į kai kuriuos prenumeratos planus, pvz., planą „Project Online Professional“ arba „Visio Online“ 2 planą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-108">„Office“ sudaro kliento programinės įrangos programos ir prisijungus naudojamos funkcijos, kurios sukurtos, kad galėtumėte kurti, bendrauti ir bendradarbiauti efektyviau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-108">Office consists of client software applications and connected experiences designed to enable you to create, communicate, and collaborate more effectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-109">Jei esate organizacijos administratorius, galite valdyti daugelį jums arba jūsų vartotojams pasiekiamų prisijungus naudojamų funkcijų, bet yra paslaugų, kurios yra būtinos, kad „Office“ veiktų, ir kurių išjungti negalima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-109">While you can control many of the connected experiences that are available to you, or to your users if you’re the admin in your organization, there are a set of services that are essential to how Office functions and therefore cannot be disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-110">Pavyzdžiui, licencijavimo paslauga, kuri patvirtina, kad turite reikiamą licenciją naudotis „Office“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-110">For example, the licensing service that confirms that you are properly licensed to use Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-111">Reikalingi tarnybų duomenys apie šias tarnybas yra renkami ir siunčiami „Microsoft“, nepaisant jokių kitų jūsų sukonfigūruotų su privatumu susijusios strategijos parametrų.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-111">Required service data about these services is collected and sent to Microsoft, regardless of any other privacy-related policy settings that you have configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-112">Šiuos duomenis galite peržiūrėti naudodami diagnostikos duomenų peržiūros programą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-112">You can see this data by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-113">Jei reikia daugiau informacijos, žr.:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-113">For more information, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-114">Reikalingi „Office“ tarnybų duomenys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-114">Required service data for Office</span></span>](required-service-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-115">Diagnostikos duomenų peržiūros programos naudojimas su „Office“</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-115">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-116">„Office“ prisijungus naudojamos funkcijos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-116">Connected experiences in Office</span></span>](connected-experiences.md)

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-117">Jei esate organizacijos administratorius, jus gali dominti šios temos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-117">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-118">„Office 365 ProPlus“ privatumo valdiklių apžvalga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-118">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-119">„Office 365 ProPlus“ privatumo valdiklių valdymas naudojant strategijos parametrus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-119">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="list-of-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-120">Pagrindinių „Office“ paslaugos sąrašas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-120">List of essential services for Office</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-121">Šioje lentelėje pateiktas pagrindinių „Office“ paslaugų sąrašas ir kiekvienos paslaugos aprašas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-121">The following table provides a list of the essential services for Office and a description of each service.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-122">**Paslauga**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-122">**Service**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-123">**Aprašas**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-123">**Description**</span></span>  |
| ------ | ---- |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-124">Autentifikavimas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-124">Authentication</span></span>](#authentication-events) | <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-125">Autentifikavimas yra keliose platformose veikianti paslauga, kurią naudojant patvirtinama jūsų „Office“ vartotojo tapatybė.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-125">Authentication is a cross-platform service that validates your Office user identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-126">Ji reikalinga, kad galėtumėte prisijungti prie „Office“, suaktyvinti „Office“ licenciją ir pasiekti debesyje saugomus failus. Ji veikia vienodai visuose „Office“ seansuose ir įrenginiuose.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-126"> It is required to enable you to sign in to Office, activate your Office license, access your files stored in the cloud, and provides a consistent experience across Office sessions and your devices.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-127">Spustelėkite ir naudokitės</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-127">Click-to-Run</span></span>](#click-to-run-events) | <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-128">Spustelėkite ir naudokitės yra diegimo technologija, naudojama diegiant ir naujinant „Office“ sistemoje „Windows“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-128">Click-to-Run is the installation technology used to install and update Office on Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-129">Ji tikrina, ar išleista naujų „Office“ versijų, o kai nauja versija pasiekiama, ją atsisiunčia ir įdiegia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-129">It checks for new versions of Office, and when a new version is available, downloads and installs it.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-130">Paslauga Spustelėkite ir naudokitės aptiks, kada reikia naujinti „Office“, atsiųs naujinimus, įskaitant saugos naujinimus, ir juos įdiegs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-130"> Click-to-Run will detect the need for, perform the download of, and install Office updates, including security updates.</span></span>     |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-131">Patobulinta konfigūravimo paslauga (ECS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-131">Enhanced Configuration Service (ECS)</span></span>](#enhanced-configuration-service-ecs-events) | <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-132">ECS suteikia „Microsoft“ galimybę perkonfigūruoti „Office“ įdiegtis, išvengiant poreikio iš naujo visuotinai įdiegti „Office“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-132">ECS provides Microsoft the ability to reconfigure Office installations without the need for you to redeploy Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-133">Ji naudojama valdyti palaipsniui diegiamas funkcijas arba naujinimus, o diegimo poveikis stebimas pagal renkamus diagnostikos duomenis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-133">It is used to control the gradual rollout of features or updates, while the impact of the rollout is monitored from diagnostic data being collected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-134">Ji taip pat naudojama siekiant sumažinti saugos arba veikimo problemas diegiant funkcijas arba naujinimus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-134">It is also used to mitigate security or performance issues with a feature or update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-135">Be to, ECS palaiko su diagnostikos duomenimis susijusius konfigūracijos keitimus, kad užtikrintų, jog būtų renkami tinkami įvykiai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-135">In addition, ECS supports configuration changes related to diagnostic data to help ensure that the appropriate events are being collected.</span></span> |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-136">Licencijavimas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-136">Licensing</span></span>](#licensing-events)     | <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-137">Licencijavimas yra debesų technologija pagrįsta paslauga, kuri palaiko naujų „Office“ įdiegčių aktyvinimą ir išlaiko licenciją įrenginiuose suaktyvinus „Office“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-137">Licensing is a cloud-based service that supports your Office activation for new installations and maintains the license on your devices after Office has been activated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-138">Ji užregistruoja visus jūsų įrenginius ir suaktyvina „Office“, patikrina „Office“ prenumeratos būseną ir valdo produktų raktus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-138">It registers each of your devices and activates Office, checks the status of your Office subscription, and manages your product keys.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-139">Paslaugų konfigūravimas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-139">Services Configuration</span></span>](#services-configuration-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-140">Paslaugų konfigūravimo paslauga suteikia galimybę naujinti „Office“ konfigūracijos parametrus ir įgalinti arba išjungti kliento funkcijas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-140">Services Configuration provides the ability to make updates to Office configuration settings to enable or disable client features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-141">Ji iškviečiama kaskart paleidus „Office“ programą ir suteikia informacijos apie kitas „Office“ konfigūracijas ir paslaugas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-141">It is called every time an Office application is started and provides details about other Office configurations and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-142">Paslaugų konfigūravimo paslauga taip pat valdo, kurios paslaugos laikomos pagrindinėmis paslaugomis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-142">Services Configuration also controls which services are designated as essential services.</span></span>  |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-143">Telemetrija </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-143">Telemetry </span></span>](#telemetry-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-144">Naudojant telemetrijos paslaugą renkami diagnostikos duomenys iš „Office“ programų.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-144">The Telemetry service is used to collect diagnostic data from Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-145">Ji suteikia galimybę rinkti „Office“ sugeneruotus diagnostikos duomenis (tiek būtinuosius, tiek pasirinktinius).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-145">It enables the collection of the diagnostic data generated by Office, both required and optional diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-146">Ji taip pat atsakinga už reikalingų „Office“ tarnybų diagnostikos duomenų dalies rinkimą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-146">It is also responsible for the collection of the service diagnostic data portion of required service data for Office.</span></span>  |

## <a name="events-and-data-fields-for-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-147">Pagrindinių „Office“ paslaugų įvykiai ir duomenų laukai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-147">Events and data fields for essential services for Office</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-148">Tolesniuose skyriuose pateikiama ši informacija:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-148">The next sections provide the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-149">Kiekvienos pagrindinės paslaugos įvykių sąrašas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-149">A list of events for each essential service</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-150">Kiekvieno įvykio aprašas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-150">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-151">Kiekvieno įvykio duomenų laukų sąrašas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-151">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-152">Kiekvieno duomenų lauko aprašas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-152">A description of each data field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-153">Šiuos įvykius galite peržiūrėti naudodami diagnostikos duomenų peržiūros programą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-153">You can see these events by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>



## <a name="authentication-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-154">Autentifikavimo įvykiai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-154">Authentication events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-155">Šie diagnostikos duomenų įvykiai renkami, kai „Office“ bando gauti autentifikavimo atpažinimo ženklą (tyliai arba pateikdamas raginimus).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-155">These diagnostic data events are collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentityfbapromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-157">Renkama, kai „Office“ rodo vartotojui formomis pagrįsto autentifikavimo prisijungimo raginimą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-157">Collected when Office shows the user a Forms-Based-Auth sign-in prompt.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-158">Kartu su tyliu atpažinimo ženklų gavimu, naudojami autentifikavimo raginimai siekiant nustatyti, ar vartotojo autentifikavimo būsena yra netinkama. Tai vartotojui iš esmės reiškia, kad kliento būsena bus Neprisijungęs, arba, blogiausiu atveju, dėl netinkamo autentifikavimo gali būti negauta licencija ir bus visiškai negalima naudoti kliento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-158">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts is used to determine if user is in a broken authentication state which, for the user, results in what is essentially an Offline Client state, or in the worst case, broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-159">Formomis pagrįsto autentifikavimo (FBA) prisijungimo raginimai naudojami kai kuriais vietinio autentifikavimo scenarijais ir paprastai norime įsitikinti, kad tai nevyksta, nes visi turėtų naudoti šiuolaikinį autentifikavimą dėl su FBA siejamų saugos pažeidžiamumų.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-159">Forms-Based-Auth (FBA) sign-in prompts are used for some on-premises authentication scenarios and typically we want to make sure this isn’t happening, as everyone should be using Modern-Auth because of security vulnerabilities associated with FBA.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-160">**Renkami šių laukų duomenys:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-160">**The following fields are collected:**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-161">**AuthScheme** – naudojama autentifikavimo schema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-161">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-162">**DocumentUrlHash** – prašomas užšifruotas URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-162">**DocumentUrlHash** - an encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-163">**EndTag** – FBA formos pabaigos žymė</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-163">**EndTag** - the tag where FBA form is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-164">**Flags** – nebenaudojama</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-164">**Flags** - Obsolete</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-165">**FlowTag** – FBA formos pradžios žymė</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-165">**FlowTag** - the tag where FBA form is started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-166">**LastError** – pateiktas klaidos kodas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-166">**LastError** – the error code returned</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-167">**PromptEndTime** – raginimo pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-167">**PromptEndTime** - the time when then prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-168">**PromptStartTime** – raginimo pradžios laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-168">**PromptStartTime** - the time when the prompt started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-169">**Result** – ar autentifikavimas sėkmingas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-169">**Result** - whether the authentication succeeded</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-170">**SessionEndTime** – įvykio seanso pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-170">**SessionEndTime** – the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-171">**Timeout** – raginimo skirtojo laiko pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-171">**Timeout** - the time when the prompt timed out</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysignoutevent"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-173">Renkama, kai vartotojas atsijungia nuo „Office“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-173">Collected when a user signs out of Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-174">Žinant, kad vartotojas atsijungė, galima klasifikuoti kitus įvykius, pvz., raginimus, kaip numatyta, kad šie įvykiai būtų tinkamai apskaičiuoti patikimumo / parengimo pateikti metrikoje ir būtų išvengta įspėjimų arba komponavimo versijų keitimų atšaukimo darant klaidingą prielaidą, kad vartotojui pateikiami netikėti prisijungimo raginimai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-174">Knowing the user is signed-out makes it possible to classify other events, such as prompts, as expected, so those events can be correctly computed in reliability / ship-readiness metrics and avoid alerting or rolling back builds on the faulty premise that the user is experiencing unexpected sign-in prompts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-175">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-175">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-176">**FlowEndTime** – atsijungimo veiksmo pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-176">**FlowEndTime** - the time when the sign out action ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-177">**FlowStartTime** – atsijungimo veiksmo pradžios laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-177">**FlowStartTime** - the time when the sign out action started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-178">**IdentityErrorState** – bet kokia tapatybės klaidos būsena atsijungiant</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-178">**IdentityErrorState** - any identity error state during sign out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** – užšifruotas tapatybės ID, kurio atsijungimo procesas vykdomas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** - the encrypted identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-180">**IdentityProviderType** – tapatybės, kurios atsijungimo procesas vykdomas, tapatybės teikėjas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-180">**IdentityProviderType** - the identity provider of the identity being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-181">**IdentityUniqueID** – tapatybės ID, kurio atsijungimo procesas vykdomas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-181">**IdentityUniqueID** - the identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-182">**SessionEndTime** – įvykio seanso pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-182">**SessionEndTime** - the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-183">**SignOutUserAction** – nurodo, kad vartotojas inicijuoja atsijungimo veiksmą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-183">**SignOutUserAction** - Indicates the user initiates the sign out action</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysspipromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-185">Renkama, kai „Office“ rodo vartotojui „Windows“ SSPI prisijungimo raginimą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-185">Collected when Office shows the user a Windows SSPI sign-in prompt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-186">Kartu su tyliu atpažinimo ženklų gavimu, autentifikavimo raginimai lemia, ar vartotojo autentifikavimo būsena yra netinkama (dėl jos kliento būsena tampa Neprisijungęs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-186">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts determine whether a user is in a broken authentication state, which results in an Offline Client state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-187">Dėl netinkamo autentifikavimo gali būti negauta licencija ir gali visiškai nepavykti naudoti kliento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-187">Broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-188">„Windows“ SSPI raginimai naudojami autentifikuojant per „Exchange“ (el. paštui sinchronizuoti), kai vartotojo „Exchange“ išteklius nebuvo nustatytas naudoti kelių dalių autentifikavimą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-188">Windows SSPI prompts are used for authenticating with Exchange (for mail synchronizing) when the user's Exchange resource hasn't been setup for multi-factor authentication.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-189">Šie įvykiai, kartu su „Office.MATS“ vardų srities įvykiais, naudojami šiais tikslais:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-189">These events, along with the Office.MATS namespace events, are used for the following purposes:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-190">1\) Siekiant nustatyti, ar klientai gali sėkmingai gauti autentifikavimo atpažinimo ženklą, ar jų autentifikavimo būsena yra netinkama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-190">1\) Identify whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-191">2\) Siekiant įvertinti, ar kliente arba paslaugose padaryti keitimai lėmė kritinį vartotojo autentifikavimo patirties ir patikimumo suprastėjimą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-191">2\) Evaluate whether changes that have occurred on the client or services have resulted in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-192">3\) Kai įvyksta triktis, šie signalai perduoda svarbius trikties kodus iš atsakingo komponento („Office“ kliento kodo, autentifikavimo bibliotekų arba tarnybų), kuriuos galima naudoti nustatant, diagnozuojant ir mažinant poveikį.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-192">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-193">4\) Šie signalai siunčiami į įvairias parengimo pateikti ir sveikatos stebėjimo programas, kurios suaktyvina įspėjimus, kad mūsų inžinieriai galėtų greitai imtis problemos sprendimo ir būtų greičiau sumažintas kritinių vartotojams dirbti neleidžiančių trikčių poveikis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-193">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical user-blocking failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-194">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-194">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-195">**AllowSavedCreds** – ar nauji kredencialai išlaikomi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-195">**AllowSavedCreds** - whether the new credential is persisted</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-196">**AuthScheme** – naudojama autentifikavimo schema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-196">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-197">**CredsSaved** – ar nauji kredencialai įrašomi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-197">**CredsSaved** - whether the new credential is saved</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-198">**DocumentUrlHash** – prašomas užšifruotas URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-198">**DocumentUrlHash** - the encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-199">**EndTag** – raginimo pabaigos žymė</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-199">**EndTag** - the tag where the prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-200">**NewIdentity**\_ErrorState – ar nauja tapatybė yra galiojanti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-200">**NewIdentity**\_ErrorState – whether the new identity is valid</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-201">**NewIdentity\_HashedUniqueId** – užšifruotas naujas tapatybės ID užbaigus raginimą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-201">**NewIdentity\_HashedUniqueId** - the encrypted new identity ID after prompt is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-202">**NewIdentity\_ProviderType** – naujas tapatybės teikėjas užbaigus raginimą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-202">**NewIdentity\_ProviderType** - the new identity provider after the prompt is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-203">**NewIdentity\_UniqueID** – naujas tapatybės ID užbaigus raginimą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-203">**NewIdentity\_UniqueID** - the new identity ID after the prompt is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-204">**OutStatus** – ar raginimo išvestis yra galiojanti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-204">**OutStatus** - whether the prompt output is valid</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-205">**PromptEndTime** - raginimo pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-205">**PromptEndTime** - the time when the prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-206">**PromptFailedTag** – žymė, nurodanti SSPI raginimo triktį</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-206">**PromptFailedTag** - the tag that indicates SSPI prompt failure</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-207">**PromptFlow** – žymė, kuri iškvietė SSPI raginimą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-207">**PromptFlow** - the tag that invoked the SSPI prompt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-208">**PromptStartTime** – raginimo pradžios laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-208">**PromptStartTime** - the time when the prompt started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-209">**Proxy** – ar naudojamas tarpinis serveris</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-209">**Proxy** - if proxy is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-210">**ServerHash** – užšifruotas serverio adresas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-210">**ServerHash** - the encrypted server address</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-211">**SessionEndTime** – įvykio seanso pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-211">**SessionEndTime** - the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-212">**Timeout** – raginimo skirtojo laiko pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-212">**Timeout** - the time when the prompt is timed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-213">**UiMessage** – vartotojo sąsajos pranešimas raginime</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-213">**UiMessage** - the UI message in the prompt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-214">**UserNameHash** – užšifruotas vartotojo vardas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-214">**UserNameHash** - the encrypted user name</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-225">**AdalWAMUsed** – žymė, kuri nurodo rezultatą, jei naudojamas ADAL-atop-WAM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-225">**AdalWAMUsed** – the tag that indicates result if ADAL-atop-WAM is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-226">**CallTag** – žymė, kuri nurodo, kas iškviečia prisijungimo vartotojo sąsają</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-226">**CallTag** – the tag that indicates the caller of sign in UI</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-227">**Context** – raginimo prisijungimo kontekstas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-227">**Context** - the sign in context for the prompt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-228">**EndTagIdentityProviderRequested** – žymė, kur prašomas tapatybės teikėjas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-228">**EndTagIdentityProviderRequested** - the tag where the identity provider is requested</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-232">**LastLoginDelta** – laiko pokytis nuo paskutinio sėkmingo prisijungimo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-232">**LastLoginDelta** - the time delta from last successful login</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-233">**NewIdentity\_ErrorState** – ar tapatybė galioja po raginimo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-233">**NewIdentity\_ErrorState** - whether the identity is valid after prompt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-237">**PromptEndTime** - raginimo pabaigos laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-237">**PromptEndTime** - the time when the prompt ended</span></span>

### <a name="officematsactionofficewin32-officematsactionofficewinrt"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-245">Tolesnis aprašas taikomas ir „Win32“, ir „WinRT“ įvykiams (pavadinimas priklauso nuo platformos)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-245">The following description applies for both Win32 and WinRT events (the name depends on platform.)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-246">„Microsoft“ autentifikavimo telemetrijos sistemos (MATS) įvykiai renkami, kai „Office“ bando gauti autentifikavimo atpažinimo ženklą (tyliai arba pateikdamas raginimus).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-246">Microsoft Auth Telemetry System (MATS) is collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-247">Kai bandymas gauti nepavyksta, įtraukiama klaidos informacija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-247">When acquisition attempts fail, error information is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-248">Šie įvykiai padeda vartotojams išvengti netinkamos autentifikavimo būsenos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-248">These events help our users avoid entering broken authentication states by:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-249">1\) Nustatant, ar klientai gali sėkmingai gauti autentifikavimo atpažinimo ženklą, ar jų autentifikavimo būsena yra netinkama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-249">1\) Identifying whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-250">2\) Įvertinant, ar kliente arba paslaugose padaryti keitimai lėmė kritinį vartotojo autentifikavimo patirties ir patikimumo suprastėjimą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-250">2\) Evaluate when changes occur on the client or services, whether they result in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-251">3\) Kai įvyksta triktis, šie signalai perduoda svarbius trikties kodus iš atsakingo komponento („Office“ kliento kodo, autentifikavimo bibliotekų arba tarnybų), kuriuos galima naudoti nustatant, diagnozuojant ir mažinant poveikį.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-251">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-252">4\) Šie signalai siunčiami į įvairias parengimo pateikti ir sveikatos stebėjimo programas, kurios suaktyvina įspėjimus, kad mūsų inžinieriai galėtų greitai imtis problemos sprendimo ir būtų greičiau sumažintas kritinių trikčių poveikis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-252">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-253">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-253">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-254">**Actiontype** – kuri autentifikavimo biblioteka naudojama</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-254">**Actiontype** - Which authentication library is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-255">**Appaudience** – ar programa sukurta vidiniam, ar išoriniam naudojimui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-255">**Appaudience** - Is the app build for internal or external use</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-256">**Appforcedprompt** – ar programa perrašė talpyklą ir priverstinai parodė raginimą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-256">**Appforcedprompt** - Did the app override cache and force a prompt to be shown</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-257">**Appname** – programos, kurią naudojant autentifikuojama, pavadinimas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-257">**Appname** - Name of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-258">**Appver** – programos, kurią naudojant identifikuojama, versija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-258">**Appver** - Version of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-259">**Askedforcreds** – ar programa paprašė vartotojo įvesti kredencialus atliekant šį veiksmą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-259">**Askedforcreds** - Did the application ask the user to enter credentials for this action</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-260">**Authoutcome** – ar autentifikavimo bandymas pavyko, nepavyko, ar buvo atšauktas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-260">**Authoutcome** - Did the authentication attempt succeed, fail, or was cancelled</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-319">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_max** – jei signalas yra agreguotas, maksimalus laikas, per kurį API atsakė ADAL, tarp visų agreguotų įvykių.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-319">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_max** - If the signal is aggregated, the max time it took ADAL to return from its API among any of the aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-321">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_sum** – jei signalas yra agreguotas, laiko, per kurį API atsakė ADAL, suma tarp visų agreguotų įvykių.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-321">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_sum** - If the signal is aggregated, the sum of the time it took ADAL to return from its API among all aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-324">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_server\_sub\_error\_code** – serverio pateiktas antrinis klaidos kodas, padedantis išsiaiškinti, kodėl nepavyko įvykdyti užklausos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-324">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_server\_sub\_error\_code** - Sub error code returned by the server to help disambiguate why the request failed.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-325">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_spe\_ring** – ar vartotojas naudojo „Secure Production Enterprise“ vidinį ratą (tik „Microsoft“ darbuotojai) (teisinga arba klaidinga).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-325">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_spe\_ring** - True/false telling if the user was using the Secure Production Enterprise inner ring (Microsoft employees only).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-326">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_start\_time** – ADAL API iškvietimo laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-326">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_start\_time** – Time the ADAL API call was made</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-330">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_tenant\_id** – GUID, identifikuojantis nuomotoją, kuriam priklauso autentifikuotas vartotojas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-330">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_tenant\_id** - GUID identifying the tenant that the authenticated user belongs to.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-331">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_acquisition\_from\_context** – apibūdina ADAL veikimo būdą pagal atpažinimo ženklus autentifikavimo kontekste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-331">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_acquisition\_from\_context** - Describes the ADAL behavior based on the tokens in the authentication context.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-332">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_type** – atnaujinimo atpažinimo ženklas (RT) arba kelių išteklių atnaujinimo atpažinimo ženklas (MRRT).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-332">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_type** – Either refresh token (RT) or multi-resource refresh token (MRRT).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-333">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_ui\_event\_count** – vartotojui rodomų raginimų skaičius.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-333">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_ui\_event\_count** - Count of prompts shown to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-334">Galėjo būti tylūs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-334">May have been silent.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-335">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_user\_cancel** – ar vartotojo sąsajos langas buvo atšauktas (teisinga arba klaidinga).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-335">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_user\_cancel** - True / false if the user interface window was cancelled.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-336">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_x\_ms\_request\_id** – papildomas užklausos ID, kurį ADAL pateikė paslaugai HTTP antraštėje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-336">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_x\_ms\_request\_id** – Additional request ID provided in HTTP header to service by ADAL.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-337">**Platform** – „Win32“ / „WinRT“ / „Android“ / „iOS“ / „Mac“</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-337">**Platform** - Win32/WinRT/Android/iOS/Mac</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-338">**Scenarioid** – GUID.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-338">**Scenarioid** – GUID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-339">Vienam scenarijui gali priklausyti keli įvykiai, pvz., scenarijus gali įtraukti naują paskyrą, bet vykstant tam scenarijui pateikiami keli raginimai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-339">Multiple events may belong to a single scenario, e.g. the scenario may be adding a new account but there are multiple prompts that occur as part of that scenario.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-340">Šis ID įgalina sąsają.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-340">This ID enables correlation to happen.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-341">**Sessionid** – GUID, identifikuojantis įkrovos seansą</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-341">**Sessionid** - GUID identifying the boot session</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-342">**Skdver** – MATS kliento SDK, naudojamo šiems duomenims sukurti, versija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-342">**Skdver** - Version of MATS client SDK used to produce this data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-343">**Starttime** – Start\*Action MATS API iškvietimo laikas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-343">**Starttime** - Time at which the Start\*Action MATS API was called</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-344">**Tenantid** – GUID, identifikuojantis nuomotoją, kuriam priklauso autentifikuotas vartotojas (ne ADAL atvejais).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-344">**Tenantid** - GUID identifying the tenant the authenticated user belongs to (in non-ADAL cases).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-345">**Uploadid** – šio įvykio unikalusis GUID, naudojamas dublikatams naikinti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-345">**Uploadid** - Unique GUID for this event, used for de-duping</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-346">**Wamapi** – identifikuoja, kuri WAM API iškviesta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-346">**Wamapi** - Identifies which WAM API is called</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** – šiuo metu nenaudojamas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** - Currently unused.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-348">Ateityje leis WAM komponentui pateikti papildomą informaciją, susijusią su autentifikavimo įvykiu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-348">In the future, allows the WAM component to dispatch additional information regarding the authentication event.</span></span>

## <a name="click-to-run-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-349">Spustelėkite ir naudokitės įvykiai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-349">Click-to-Run events</span></span>

### <a name="officeclicktorunbootstrapper"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-350">Office.ClickToRun.Bootstrapper</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-350">Office.ClickToRun.Bootstrapper</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-351">„Office“ sąrankos ir aprašų duomenys, renkami vartotojui paleidus „Office“ setup.exe, kad modifikuotų įdiegtus „Office“ produktus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-351">Office set up and inventory data collected when the user is running Office setup.exe to modify their installed Office products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-352">Naudojami vertinant viso vartotojo inicijuoto „Office“ diegimo sėkmingumą, įskaitant būtinąsias patikras.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-352">Used to measure success / failure of a full user-initiated Office installation including pre-requisite checks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-353">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-353">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-354">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorCode** – įvykusios klaidos kodas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-354">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorCode** – The error code we failed with</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-355">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorSource** – funkcija, kurios klaida įvyko</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-355">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorSource** – The function we failed in</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-356">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_FailingState** – įkėlimo įrankio dalis, kurioje įvyko klaida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-356">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_FailingState** – The part that we failed in the boostrapperbootstrapper</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-357">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_OExceptionType** – išimties tipas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-357">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_OExceptionType** – The type of exception we failed with</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-358">**Data\_Culture** – kultūra, su kuria vykdomas šis „exe“, pvz., „en-us“</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-358">**Data\_Culture** - the culture we are running this exe with, i.e. en-us</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-359">**Data\_HashedOLSToken** – atpažinimo ženklo SHA-256 maiša, kurią mums nurodo OLS paslauga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-359">**Data\_HashedOLSToken** - a sha-256 hash of a token the OLS service gives us</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-360">**Data\_Platform** – „x64“ arba „x86“ įdiegtis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-360">**Data\_Platform** - x64 or x86 install</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-361">**Data\_PrereqFailure\_Type** – įvykusi būtinųjų sąlygų triktis, pvz., nepalaikoma operacinė sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-361">**Data\_PrereqFailure\_Type** – The prerequisite failure we hit, ie. the operating system is not supported</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-362">**Data\_ProductReleaseId** – diegiamas produktas, pvz., „Office 365 ProPlus“</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-362">**Data\_ProductReleaseId** - Product we’re installing, i.e. Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>

### <a name="officeclicktoruncorruptioncheck"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-363">Office.ClickToRun.CorruptionCheck</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-363">Office.ClickToRun.CorruptionCheck</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-364">„Office“ sąrankos ir inventoriaus duomenys, renkami Spustelėkite ir naudokitės klientui vykdant patikrą dėl sugadinimo, siekiant įsitikinti, kad „Office“ dvejetainiai failai yra teisingi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-364">Office set up and inventory data collected when Click-to-Run client is running a corruption check to make sure that Office binaries are correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-365">Naudojami vertinant, ar „Office“ dvejetainiai failai yra sugadinti ir kurie dvejetainiai failai yra sugadinti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-365">Used to measure corruption of Office binaries, and which binaries are corrupt.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-370">**Data\_AddFileCount –** kiek failų įtraukiame</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-370">**Data\_AddFileCount -** how many files we’re adding</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-377">**Data\_CorruptVersionFiles –** failų, kurių versija sugadinta, imtis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-377">**Data\_CorruptVersionFiles -** a sample of the files that have a corrupted version</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-378">**Data\_FileBadDigestCount –** kiek failų nepavyko atidaryti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-378">**Data\_FileBadDigestCount -** how many files we failed to open</span></span>

### <a name="officeclicktorunmachinemetadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-406">Office.ClickToRun.MachineMetadata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-406">Office.ClickToRun.MachineMetadata</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-410">**Data\_OfficeBitness** – sistemos, kurioje įdiegtas „Office“, bitų skaičius (x86 arba x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-410">**Data\_OfficeBitness** – The bitness that Office is installed in, x86 or x64</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-413">**Data\_SqmMachineID** – unikalusis kompiuterio ID, kurį naudoja „Windows SQM Data“\_SusClientID – kompiuterio „Office“ naujinimo identifikatoriaus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-413">**Data\_SqmMachineID** – Unique Machine ID used by Windows SQM Data\_SusClientID- Machine Office update identifier</span></span>

### <a name="officeclicktorunodt"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-414">Office.ClickToRun.ODT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-414">Office.ClickToRun.ODT</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-415">„Office“ sąrankos ir inventoriaus duomenys, renkami, kai IT administratorius vykdo „Office“ diegimo įrankio Spustelėkite ir naudokitės setup.exe, kad modifikuotų vartotojų įdiegtus „Office“ produktus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-415">Office set up and inventory data collected when an IT Admin is running the Office Deployment Tool Click-to-Run setup.exe to modify their users’ installed Office products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-416">Naudojamas vertinant visų IT administratoriaus inicijuotų „Office“ diegimų sėkmingumą, įskaitant būtinųjų sąlygų patikras.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-416">It is used to measure success / failure of full IT Admin initiated Office installations including pre-requisite checks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-417">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-417">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-418">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorCode –** įvykusios klaidos kodas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-418">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorCode-** The error code we failed with</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-419">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorSource –** funkcija, kurios klaida įvyko</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-419">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_ErrorSource-** The function we failed in</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-420">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_FailingState –** įkėlimo įrankio dalis, kurioje įvyko klaida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-420">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_FailingState-** The part that we failed in the boot-strapper</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-1389">**Count** – užklaustų funkcijų prievadų skaičius šiame paketiniame įvykyje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-1389">**Count** - Number of queried feature gates in this batched event</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-1390">**Features** – informacija apie užklaustą prievadą.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-1390">**Features** - Information about the queried gate.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-1391">**Sequence** – FeatureGate užklausimo tvarka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-1391">**Sequence** - Order in which FeatureGate was queried</span></span>

### <a name="officeexperimentationflightnumberline"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-1392">Office.Experimentation.FlightNumberLine</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-1392">Office.Experimentation.FlightNumberLine</span></span>

### <a name="officelicensingactivation"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-1407">Office.Licensing.Activation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-1407">Office.Licensing.Activation</span></span>

### <a name="officelicensingheartbeat"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-1448">Office.Licensing.Heartbeat</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-1448">Office.Licensing.Heartbeat</span></span>

### <a name="officelicensinginstallkey"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-1463">Office.Licensing.InstallKey</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-1463">Office.Licensing.InstallKey</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetryvolumetrackingdata"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2367">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2367">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2368">Telemetrjos įvykių kiekio stebėjimo metrika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2368">Event volume tracking metrics for telemetry events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2369">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2369">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2370">**EventThreshold** – didžiausias vieno įvykio egzempliorių, kuriuos galima išsiųsti laikotarpiu, skaičius.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2370">**EventThreshold** - The maximum number of instances of a single event that can be sent in a window of time.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2371">**HighestEventCount** – didžiausias vieno įvykio egzempliorių, išsiųstų šiuo laikotarpiu, skaičius.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2371">**HighestEventCount** - The highest number of instances of a single event sent this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2372">**HighestEventName** – įvykio, kurio egzempliorių skaičius šiuo laikotarpiu didžiausias, skaičius.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2372">**HighestEventName** - The name of the event with the highest number of instances in this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2373">**TimeWindowInSeconds** – laikotarpio trukmė sekundėmis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2373">**TimeWindowInSeconds** - The duration of the window in seconds.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2374">**TotalEvents** – bendras įvykių, išsiųstų laikotarpiu, skaičius.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2374">**TotalEvents** - The total number of events sent during the window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2375">**UniqueEvents** – unikalių įvykių, išsiųstų laikotarpiu, skaičius.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2375">**UniqueEvents** - The number of unique events sent during a window.</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetrywritepayloadstodisk"></a><span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2376">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2376">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2377">Tikrina, ar tam tikros senstelėjusio srauto dalys veikia platformose, kuriose jis dar naudojamas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2377">Verifies certain parts of legacy pipeline are working on platforms that still use it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2378">Renkami šių laukų duomenys:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2378">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bd78e-2379">**DetachedDuration** – atjungties trukmė mikrosekundėmis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bd78e-2379">**DetachedDuration** - Detached duration in microseconds</span></span>
